    FROM [Rent] AS [r]
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Estate] AS [e] ON [t].[EstateId] = [e].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [File] AS [f] ON [t].[Id] = [f].[RentId]
LEFT JOIN [Tenant] AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[RentId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [e].[Id], [f].[Id]
